<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугивать.html>запу́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapúgivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугивание.html>запу́гивание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapúgivanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугивание.html>запу́гивания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугивание.html>запу́гивания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугивание.html>запу́гиваний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запугивать.html>запу́гивающий</a> (22298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***запускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запускать.html>запуска́ть</a> (8550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запускать.html>запуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запустить.html>запусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to launch (a missile, rocket, a probe, etc.)</li>
<li>to launch; to start (operation or manufacturing of something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:модель.html>моде́ль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запущенный.html>запу́щена</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvaja modɛ́lʹ avtomobílja <b>zapúščena</b> v proizvódstvo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Production of the new car model has been started.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let in</li>
<li>to neglect, to fail to take care of, to let something decline or decay; to abandon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запущенный.html>запу́щена</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Boléznʹ bylá sílʹno zapúščena.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Disease was left untreated until the late stage.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запуск.html>за́пуск</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zápusk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запустить.html>запу́щенный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapúščennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***запустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запустить.html>запусти́ть</a> (4383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запустить.html>запусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запускать.html>запуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to launch (a missile, rocket, a probe, etc.)</li>
<li>to launch; to start (operation or manufacturing of something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:модель.html>моде́ль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запущенный.html>запу́щена</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvaja modɛ́lʹ avtomobílja <b>zapúščena</b> v proizvódstvo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Production of the new car model has been started.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let in</li>
<li>to neglect, to fail to take care of, to let something decline or decay; to abandon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запущенный.html>запу́щена</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Boléznʹ bylá sílʹno <b>zapúščena</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Disease was left untreated until the late stage.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***запутать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a> (13279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapútatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to entangle, to tangle</li>
<li>to tangle, to confuse, to complicate, to muddle up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapútatʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to complicate matters; muddle a business; make a mess of a business; get things into a muddle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get entangled/enmeshed <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>Будь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осторожный.html>осторо́жен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тали</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> какую-нибудь <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рию</a>. </span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́таться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapútatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутываться.html>запу́тываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get tangled/entangled/enmeshed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бечевка.html>бечёвка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́талась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bečóvka <b>zapútalasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the string has got tangled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become more confused/complicated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be misled, to get confused, to get mixed up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get entangled/enmeshed <i>(in, by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́таться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:финансовый.html>фина́нсовых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудность.html>тру́дностях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zapútatʹsja</b> v finánsovyx trúdnostjax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be enmeshed by financial difficulties</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывавший</a> (30560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapútyvavšij</span>)

***запутывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывать</a> (30560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapútyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to entangle, to tangle</li>
<li>to tangle, to confuse, to complicate, to muddle up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get entangled/enmeshed <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

***запутываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запутываться.html>запу́тываться</a> (25529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapútyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутываться.html>запу́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapútyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́таться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get tangled/entangled/enmeshed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бечевка.html>бечёвка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́тается</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bečóvka <b>zapútajetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the string is getting tangled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become more confused/complicated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be misled, to get confused, to get mixed up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутывать.html>запу́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapútyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>abandoned, neglected</li></ol>

***запыхаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запыхаться.html>запыхаться</a> (8912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запыхаться.html>запыха́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapyxátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запыхаться.html>запы́хаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapýxatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be out of breath from exertion (e.g. fast walking)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запята́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapjatája</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запято́й</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запяты́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запяты́х</a></b>)

***запятнать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запятнать.html>запятна́ть</a> (26056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пятна́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatnátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запятнать.html>запятна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapjatnátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stain, to soil</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disgrace, to defame</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to touch or hit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in games of tag or lapta</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mark, to stamp, to brand</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятно.html>пятно́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pjatnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:оставить.html>оста́вив</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятно.html>пятна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чём-либо, <a href = vnd.unilang:запачкать.html>запа́чкать</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заработать.html>зарабо́тать</a> (2646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заработать.html>зарабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарабатывать.html>зараба́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to earn</li>
<li>to start to work</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заработный.html>за́работный</a> (11489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заработать.html>зарабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with unexpected stress shift.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заработный.html>за́работный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zárabotnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wages, salary; earned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заработный.html>за́работная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плат.html>пла́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zárabotnaja pláta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wages, salary</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заработок.html>за́работок</a> (5981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заработать.html>зарабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
